1d:["$","p",null,{"style":{"fontSize":"1rem","color":"var(--text-body)","lineHeight":1.75,"marginBottom":"1.25em","marginTop":0},"children":["using the model in place of real environment steps. If the model is accurate, imagined\ntrajectories provide the same learning signal as real ones at a fraction of the\nwall-clock cost.
